<td><a href="/wiki/Unix_time" title="Unix time">Unix time</a></td>
<td>31536000 – 63071999</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div class="plainlinks hlist navbar"><span style="word-spacing:0">This box:</span>

<li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Year_in_various_calendars&amp;action=edit"><span title="Edit this template">edit</span></a></li>

<table class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" role="presentation" style="border:1px solid #aaa;background-color:#f9f9f9">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Commons-logo.svg"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1971" title="commons:Category:1971">1971</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1971 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMLXXI</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Friday" title="Common year starting on Friday">starting on Friday</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dominical_letter" title="Dominical letter">dominical letter</a> C) of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1971st year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 971st year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd millennium</a>, the 71st year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th century</a>, and the 2nd year of the <a href="/wiki/1970s" title="1970s">1970s</a> decade.</p>
<p>The world population increased by 2.1% this year; the highest in history.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_2" title="January 2">January 2</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/1971_Ibrox_disaster" title="1971 Ibrox disaster">Ibrox disaster</a>: A stairway crush at the Rangers vs. Celtic <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> match in <a href="/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">Glasgow</a>, Scotland, kills 66.</li>
<li>A ban on radio and television <a href="/wiki/Cigarette" title="Cigarette">cigarette</a> advertisements goes into effect in the United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_3" title="January 3">January 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> <a href="/wiki/Open_University" title="Open University">Open University</a> begins in the United Kingdom.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_5" title="January 5">January 5</a> – The 1st ever <a href="/wiki/One_Day_International" title="One Day International">ODI cricket</a> match is played between Australia &amp; England at the M.C.G.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_8" title="January 8">January 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Tupamaros" title="Tupamaros">Tupamaros</a> kidnap Geoffrey Jackson, British ambassador to <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Montevideo" title="Montevideo">Montevideo</a>, keeping him captive until September.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_9" title="January 9">January 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguayan</a> president <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Pacheco_Areco" title="Jorge Pacheco Areco">Jorge Pacheco Areco</a> demands emergency powers for 90 days due to kidnappings, and receives them the next day.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> – The landmark television sitcom <i><a href="/wiki/All_in_the_Family" title="All in the Family">All in the Family</a></i>, starring <a href="/wiki/Carroll_O%27Connor" title="Carroll O'Connor">Carroll O'Connor</a> as <a href="/wiki/Archie_Bunker" title="Archie Bunker">Archie Bunker</a>, debuts on <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">CBS</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_14" title="January 14">January 14</a> – Seventy <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> political prisoners are released in <a href="/wiki/Santiago" title="Santiago">Santiago</a>, Chile; Giovanni Enrico Bucher is released <a href="/wiki/January_16" title="January 16">January 16</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aswan_High_Dam" title="Aswan High Dam">Aswan High Dam</a> officially opens in Egypt.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_18" title="January 18">January 18</a> – Strikes in Poland demand the resignation of Interior Minister <a href="/wiki/Kazimierz_%C5%9Awita%C5%82a" title="Kazimierz Świtała">Kazimierz Świtała</a>. He resigns January 23 and is replaced by Franciszek Szlachcic.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_19" title="January 19">January 19</a> – Representatives of 23 western oil companies begin negotiations with <a href="/wiki/OPEC" title="OPEC">OPEC</a> in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> to stabilize <a href="/wiki/Petroleum" title="Petroleum">oil</a> prices; <a href="/wiki/February_14" title="February 14">February 14</a> they sign a treaty with 6 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Khalij_el-Arab" title="Khalij el-Arab">Khalij el-Arab</a> countries.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_24" title="January 24">January 24</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Guinea" title="Guinea">Guinean</a> government sentences to death 92 Guineans who helped Portuguese troops in the failed landing attempts in November <a href="/wiki/1970" title="1970">1970</a>; 72 are sentenced to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hard_labor" title="Hard labor">hard labor</a> for life; 58 of the sentenced are hanged the next day.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>, <a href="/wiki/Idi_Amin" title="Idi Amin">Idi Amin</a> deposes <a href="/wiki/Milton_Obote" title="Milton Obote">Milton Obote</a> in a coup, and becomes president.</li>
<li>In Los Angeles, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Manson" title="Charles Manson">Charles Manson</a> and 3 female "Family" members are found guilty of the 1969 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tate%E2%80%93LaBianca_murders" title="Tate–LaBianca murders">Tate–LaBianca murders</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Himachal_Pradesh" title="Himachal Pradesh">Himachal Pradesh</a> becomes the 18th Indian state.</li>
<li><i>Intelsat IV</i> (F2) is launched; it enters commercial service over the Atlantic Ocean <a href="/wiki/March_26" title="March 26">March 26</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_31" title="January 31">January 31</a> – <a href="/wiki/Apollo_program" title="Apollo program">Apollo program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_14" title="Apollo 14">Apollo 14</a></i> (carrying astronauts <a href="/wiki/Alan_Shepard" title="Alan Shepard">Alan Shepard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stuart_Roosa" title="Stuart Roosa">Stuart Roosa</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Edgar_Mitchell" title="Edgar Mitchell">Edgar Mitchell</a>) lifts off on the third successful lunar landing mission.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg/220px-AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg/330px-AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg/440px-AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AswanHighDam_Egypt.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/January_15" title="January 15">January 15</a>: <a href="/wiki/Aswan_Dam" title="Aswan Dam">Aswan Dam</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_4" title="February 4">February 4</a> – In Britain, <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Limited" title="Rolls-Royce Limited">Rolls-Royce</a> goes bankrupt and is nationalised.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_14" title="Apollo 14">Apollo 14</a></i> lands on the Moon.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_7" title="February 7">February 7</a>
<ul>
<li>An earthquake in the city of <a href="/wiki/Tuscania" title="Tuscania">Tuscania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> kills 31.</li>
<li>Switzerland gives women voting rights in state elections, but not in all <a href="/wiki/Cantons_of_Switzerland" title="Cantons of Switzerland">canton</a>-specific ones.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/W%C5%82adys%C5%82aw_Gomu%C5%82ka" title="Władysław Gomułka">Władysław Gomułka</a> is expelled from the Central Council of the Polish Communist Party.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_8" title="February 8">February 8</a> – A new <a href="/wiki/Stock_market_index" title="Stock market index">stock market index</a> called the <a href="/wiki/Nasdaq_Composite" title="Nasdaq Composite">Nasdaq Composite</a> debuts.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_9" title="February 9">February 9</a>
<ul>
<li>The 6.5–6.7 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">Mw</a> <a href="/wiki/1971_San_Fernando_earthquake" title="1971 San Fernando earthquake">Sylmar earthquake</a> hits the <a href="/wiki/Greater_Los_Angeles_Area" title="Greater Los Angeles Area">Greater Los Angeles Area</a> with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of XI (<i>Extreme</i>), killing 64 and injuring 2,000.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Satchel_Paige" title="Satchel Paige">Satchel Paige</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Negro_league_baseball" title="Negro league baseball">Negro League</a> player to become voted into the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baseball_Hall_of_Fame" title="Baseball Hall of Fame">Baseball Hall of Fame</a> from the Negro League.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Apollo_program" title="Apollo program">Apollo program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_14" title="Apollo 14">Apollo 14</a></i> returns to Earth after the third manned Moon landing.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_11" title="February 11">February 11</a> – The US, UK, USSR and others sign the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seabed_Treaty" title="Seabed Treaty">Seabed Treaty</a>, outlawing <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_weapon" title="Nuclear weapon">nuclear weapons</a> on the ocean floor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_11" title="February 11">February 11</a>–<a href="/wiki/February_12" title="February 12">February 12</a> – Palestinian and Jordanian fighters clash in <a href="/wiki/Amman" title="Amman">Amman</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_13" title="February 13">February 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>: Backed by American air and artillery support, <a href="/wiki/South_Vietnam" title="South Vietnam">South Vietnamese</a> troops invade <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Laos" title="Kingdom of Laos">Laos</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_15" title="February 15">February 15</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Decimal_Day" title="Decimal Day">Decimal Day</a>: – The United Kingdom and Ireland both switch to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Decimal_currency" title="Decimal currency">decimal currency</a> (see also <a href="/wiki/Decimalisation" title="Decimalisation">decimalisation</a>).</li>
<li>Protesting Belgian farmers bring 3 live cows to crash the <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Community" title="European Economic Community">EEC</a> meeting in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_16" title="February 16">February 16</a> – In Italy, a local parliament elects the city of <a href="/wiki/Catanzaro" title="Catanzaro">Catanzaro</a> as the capital of <a href="/wiki/Calabria" title="Calabria">Calabria</a>; residents of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reggio_di_Calabria" title="Reggio di Calabria">Reggio di Calabria</a> riot for 5 days because of the decision.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_20" title="February 20">February 20</a>
<ul>
<li>Fifty <a href="/wiki/Tornado" title="Tornado">tornadoes</a> rage in <a href="/wiki/Mississippi" title="Mississippi">Mississippi</a>, killing 74 people.</li>
<li>The U.S. <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Broadcast_System" title="Emergency Broadcast System">Emergency Broadcast System</a> sends an erroneous warning, meant to be a standard weekly test conducted by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NORAD" title="NORAD">NORAD</a> in Cheyenne Mountain in Colorado; many radio stations just ignore it. The most notorious warning was of <a href="/wiki/WOWO_(AM)" title="WOWO (AM)">WOWO (AM)</a> in <a href="/wiki/Fort_Wayne,_Indiana" title="Fort Wayne, Indiana">Fort Wayne, Indiana</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_21" title="February 21">February 21</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Convention_on_Psychotropic_Substances" title="Convention on Psychotropic Substances">Convention on Psychotropic Substances</a> is signed at <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_26" title="February 26">February 26</a> – Secretary General <a href="/wiki/U_Thant" title="U Thant">U Thant</a> signs the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> proclamation of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vernal_equinox" title="Vernal equinox">vernal equinox</a> as <a href="/wiki/Earth_Day" title="Earth Day">Earth Day</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_27" title="February 27">February 27</a> – Doctors in the first Dutch <a href="/wiki/Abortion_clinic" title="Abortion clinic">abortion clinic</a> (Mildredhuis in <a href="/wiki/Arnhem" title="Arnhem">Arnhem</a>) start to perform <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abortus_provocatus" title="Abortus provocatus">abortus provocatus</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_28" title="February 28">February 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Evel_Knievel" title="Evel Knievel">Evel Knievel</a> sets a world record and jumps 19 cars in <a href="/wiki/Ontario,_California" title="Ontario, California">Ontario, California</a>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2359" data-file-width="2340" height="222" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg/220px-Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg/330px-Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg/440px-Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Apollo_14_Shepard.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a>: <a href="/wiki/Apollo_14" title="Apollo 14">Apollo 14</a> on Moon</div>
</div>
</div>
