<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_1" title="March 1">March 1</a>
<ul>
<li>A bomb explodes in the men's room at the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol" title="United States Capitol">United States Capitol</a>; the <a href="/wiki/Weather_Underground" title="Weather Underground">Weather Underground</a> claims responsibility.</li>
<li>Pakistani President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Agha_Muhammad_Yahya_Khan" title="Agha Muhammad Yahya Khan">Agha Muhammad Yahya Khan</a> indefinitely postpones the pending National Assembly session, precipitating massive civil disobedience in <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a>.</li>
<li>Canadian <a href="/wiki/John_Robarts" title="John Robarts">John Robarts</a> ends his term of office as the 17th <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_Ontario" title="Premier of Ontario">Premier of Ontario</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_4" title="March 4">March 4</a> – The southern part of <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">Quebec</a>, and especially <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">Montreal</a>, receive 16½" (42 cm) of snow in what becomes known as the <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Canadian_blizzard_of_March_1971" title="Eastern Canadian blizzard of March 1971">Century's Snowstorm</a> (<i>la tempête du siècle</i>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_5" title="March 5">March 5</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> army occupies <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a>. In <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">Belfast</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Led_Zeppelin" title="Led Zeppelin">Led Zeppelin</a> show includes the first public performance of <a href="/wiki/Stairway_to_Heaven" title="Stairway to Heaven">Stairway to Heaven</a>, a song from the <a href="/wiki/Led_Zeppelin_IV" title="Led Zeppelin IV">fourth album</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_6" title="March 6">March 6</a> – A fire in a mental hospital at <a href="/wiki/Burgh%C3%B6lzli" title="Burghölzli">Burghölzli</a>, Switzerland, kills 28 people.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_7" title="March 7">March 7</a>
<ul>
<li>The British postal workers' strike, led by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_of_Post_Office_Workers" title="Union of Post Office Workers">UPW</a> General Secretary <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Jackson_(trade_unionist)" title="Thomas Jackson (trade unionist)">Tom Jackson</a>, ends after 47 days.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Mujibur_Rahman" title="Sheikh Mujibur Rahman">Sheikh Mujibur Rahman</a>, political leader of then <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a> (present day-<a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>), delivers his famous speech in the Racecourse Field in <a href="/wiki/Dhaka" title="Dhaka">Dhaka</a>, calling on the masses to be prepared to fight for national independence.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_8" title="March 8">March 8</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Citizens%27_Commission_to_Investigate_the_FBI" title="Citizens' Commission to Investigate the FBI">Citizens' Commission to Investigate the FBI</a> breaks into the <a href="/wiki/Media,_Pennsylvania" title="Media, Pennsylvania">Media, Pennsylvania</a> offices of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">Federal Bureau of Investigation</a> and removes all the files.</li>
<li>'<a href="/wiki/Fight_of_the_Century" title="Fight of the Century">Fight of the Century</a>': Boxer <a href="/wiki/Joe_Frazier" title="Joe Frazier">Joe Frazier</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Muhammad_Ali" title="Muhammad Ali">Muhammad Ali</a> at <a href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden" title="Madison Square Garden">Madison Square Garden</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hafez_al-Assad" title="Hafez al-Assad">Hafez al-Assad</a> becomes president of <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_12" title="March 12">March 12</a>–<a href="/wiki/March_13" title="March 13">March 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/The_Allman_Brothers_Band" title="The Allman Brothers Band">The Allman Brothers Band</a> plays their legendary concert at the <a href="/wiki/Fillmore_East" title="Fillmore East">Fillmore East</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_16" title="March 16">March 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Trygve_Bratteli" title="Trygve Bratteli">Trygve Bratteli</a> forms a government in Norway.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_18" title="March 18">March 18</a> – A landslide at Chungar, <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a> crashes into <a href="/wiki/Yanawayin_Lake" title="Yanawayin Lake">Yanawayin Lake</a>, killing 200.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_23" title="March 23">March 23</a> – General <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alejandro_Lanusse" title="Alejandro Lanusse">Alejandro Lanusse</a> of <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> takes power in a military coup.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_25" title="March 25">March 25</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> army starts <a href="/wiki/Operation_Searchlight" title="Operation Searchlight">Operation Searchlight</a> in <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a> from midnight, after President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Agha_Muhammad_Yahya_Khan" title="Agha Muhammad Yahya Khan">Agha Muhammad Yahya Khan</a>, a military ruler, voids election results that gave the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Awami_League" title="Awami League">Awami League</a> an overwhelming majority in the parliament.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_26" title="March 26">March 26</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>) independence is declared by Sheikh Mujibur Rahman and transmitted using <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/East_Pakistan_Rifles" title="East Pakistan Rifles">East Pakistan Rifles</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Border_Guards_Bangladesh" title="Border Guards Bangladesh">Border Guards Bangladesh</a>) radio.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nihat_Erim" title="Nihat Erim">Nihat Erim</a> (a former <a href="/wiki/Republican_People%27s_Party_(Turkey)" title="Republican People's Party (Turkey)">CHP</a> member) forms the new government of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> (33rd government,composed mostly of technocrats).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_27" title="March 27">March 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>) independence is repeatedly declared by Army Major (later President of Bangladesh) <a href="/wiki/Ziaur_Rahman" title="Ziaur Rahman">Ziaur Rahman</a> on behalf of Sheikh Mujibur Rahman from Kalurghat Radio Station, <a href="/wiki/Chittagong" title="Chittagong">Chittagong</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_28" title="March 28">March 28</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/The_Ed_Sullivan_Show" title="The Ed Sullivan Show">The Ed Sullivan Show</a></i> airs its final episode.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_29" title="March 29">March 29</a>
<ul>
<li>U.S. Army Lieutenant <a href="/wiki/William_Calley" title="William Calley">William Calley</a> is found guilty of 22 murders in the <a href="/wiki/My_Lai_Massacre" title="My Lai Massacre">My Lai Massacre</a> and sentenced to life in prison (he is later pardoned).</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a> jury recommends the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Death_penalty" title="Death penalty">death penalty</a> for <a href="/wiki/Charles_Manson" title="Charles Manson">Charles Manson</a> and 3 female followers.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_1" title="April 1">April 1</a> – The United Kingdom lifts all restrictions on gold ownership.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_5" title="April 5">April 5</a>
<ul>
<li>In <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylon" title="Ceylon">Ceylon</a>, a group calling themselves the <a href="/wiki/Janatha_Vimukthi_Peramuna" title="Janatha Vimukthi Peramuna">People’s Liberation Front</a> begins a rebellion against the <a href="/wiki/Sirimavo_Bandaranaike" title="Sirimavo Bandaranaike">Bandaranaike</a> government.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> and <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">East Germany</a> establish <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Diplomatic_relations" title="Diplomatic relations">diplomatic relations</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mount_Etna" title="Mount Etna">Mount Etna</a> erupts in Sicily.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_7" title="April 7">April 7</a> – Greece releases 261 <a href="/wiki/Political_prisoner" title="Political prisoner">political prisoners</a>, 50 of whom are sent into internal exile.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_8" title="April 8">April 8</a> – A right-wing coup attempt is exposed in <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_9" title="April 9">April 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/Charles_Manson" title="Charles Manson">Charles Manson</a> is sentenced to death; in 1972, the sentence for all California Death Row inmates is commuted to life imprisonment.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_12" title="April 12">April 12</a> – Palestinians retreat from <a href="/wiki/Amman" title="Amman">Amman</a> to the north of <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_17" title="April 17">April 17</a>
<ul>
<li>The People's Republic of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> forms, under <a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Mujibur_Rahman" title="Sheikh Mujibur Rahman">Sheikh Mujibur Rahman</a>, at Mujibnagor.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> sign an agreement to form a <a href="/wiki/Confederation" title="Confederation">confederation</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_19" title="April 19">April 19</a>
<ul>
<li>The government of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> flees to India.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a> becomes a <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a>.</li>
<li>The Soviet Union launches <i><a href="/wiki/Salyut_1" title="Salyut 1">Salyut 1</a></i>.</li>
<li>Followers of <a href="/wiki/Charles_Manson" title="Charles Manson">Charles Manson</a>, the Manson Family, are sentenced to the gas chamber.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_20" title="April 20">April 20</a>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Swann_v._Charlotte-Mecklenburg_Board_of_Education" title="Swann v. Charlotte-Mecklenburg Board of Education">Swann v. Charlotte-Mecklenburg Board of Education</a></i>: The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court of the United States</a> rules unanimously that busing of students may be ordered to achieve racial <a href="/wiki/Desegregation" title="Desegregation">desegregation</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodian</a> Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Lon_Nol" title="Lon Nol">Lon Nol</a> resigns, but remains effectively in power until the next elections.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_21" title="April 21">April 21</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Siaka_Stevens" title="Siaka Stevens">Siaka Stevens</a> is elected the first president of <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Duvalier" title="François Duvalier">François Duvalier</a>, president of <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, dies; his son <a href="/wiki/Jean-Claude_Duvalier" title="Jean-Claude Duvalier">Jean-Claude Duvalier</a> follows him as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President-for-life" title="President-for-life">president-for-life</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_24" title="April 24">April 24</a>
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Soyuz_10" title="Soyuz 10">Soyuz 10</a></i> docks with <i><a href="/wiki/Salyut_1" title="Salyut 1">Salyut 1</a></i>.</li>
<li>Five hundred thousand people in Washington, D.C. and 125,000 in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a> march in protest against the <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_25" title="April 25">April 25</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Todor_Zhivkov" title="Todor Zhivkov">Todor Zhivkov</a> is re-elected as the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgarian</a> Communist Party.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Franz_Jonas" title="Franz Jonas">Franz Jonas</a> is re-elected as president of Austria.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_26" title="April 26">April 26</a> – The government of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> declares a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_of_siege" title="State of siege">state of siege</a> in 11 provinces, <a href="/wiki/Ankara" title="Ankara">Ankara</a> included, due to violent <a href="/wiki/Demonstration_(protest)" title="Demonstration (protest)">demonstrations</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_28" title="April 28">April 28</a> – The first number of <i>Il Manifesto</i> is issued in Italy.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_29" title="April 29">April 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> nationalizes the American-owned Matilde zinc mine.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_30" title="April 30">April 30</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Milwaukee_Bucks" title="Milwaukee Bucks">Milwaukee Bucks</a> win the <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">NBA</a> World Championship, sweeping the <a href="/wiki/Washington_Wizards" title="Washington Wizards">Baltimore Bullets</a> in 4 straight games.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_1" title="May 1">May 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">Amtrak</a> begins inter-city rail passenger service in the United States.</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylon" title="Ceylon">Ceylonese</a> government promises <a href="/wiki/Amnesty" title="Amnesty">amnesty</a> for those guerillas who surrender before <a href="/wiki/April_5" title="April 5">April 5</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_2" title="May 2">May 2</a> – In <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylon" title="Ceylon">Ceylon</a>, left-wing guerillas launch a series of assaults against public buildings.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_3" title="May 3">May 3</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal F.C.</a> wins the English Division 1 <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> league championship at the home of their bitter rivals, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur" title="Tottenham Hotspur">Tottenham Hotspur</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Ray_Kennedy" title="Ray Kennedy">Ray Kennedy</a> scoring the winner. (Arsenal FC will go on to win the league and cup 'double' 6 days later by defeating <a href="/wiki/Liverpool" title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a> in the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> final).</li>
<li>The Harris Poll claims that 60% of Americans are against the <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>.</li>
<li>East German leader <a href="/wiki/Walter_Ulbricht" title="Walter Ulbricht">Walter Ulbricht</a> resigns as Communist Party leader but retains the position of head of state.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1971_May_Day_Protests" title="1971 May Day Protests">1971 May Day Protests</a>: Anti-war militants attempt to disrupt government business in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>; police and military units arrest as many as 12,000, most of whom are later released.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_5" title="May 5">May 5</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_dollar" title="US dollar">US dollar</a> floods the European <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Currency_market" title="Currency market">currency markets</a> and threatens especially the <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Mark" title="Deutsche Mark">Deutsche Mark</a>; the central banks of Austria, Belgium, Netherlands and Switzerland stop the currency trading.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_6" title="May 6">May 6</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ceylon" title="Ceylon">Ceylon</a> government begins a major offensive against the <a href="/wiki/Janatha_Vimukthi_Peramuna" title="Janatha Vimukthi Peramuna">People's Liberation Front</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_9" title="May 9">May 9</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arsenal_FC" title="Arsenal FC">Arsenal FC</a> beats <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool F.C.</a> 2-1 to win the English <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a>, thus completing the league and cup 'double'.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mariner_8" title="Mariner 8">Mariner 8</a> fails to launch.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_12" title="May 12">May 12</a> – An <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> destroys most of the city of <a href="/wiki/Burdur" title="Burdur">Burdur</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_15" title="May 15">May 15</a> – Efraim Elrom, <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> ambassador to Turkey, is kidnapped; he is found killed in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> <a href="/wiki/May_25" title="May 25">May 25</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_16" title="May 16">May 16</a> – A coup attempt is exposed and foiled in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_18" title="May 18">May 18</a>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. Congress formally votes to end funding for the American Supersonic Transport program.</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Montr%C3%A9al_Canadiens" title="Montréal Canadiens">Montréal Canadiens</a> win the <a href="/wiki/Stanley_Cup" title="Stanley Cup">Stanley Cup</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Blackhawks" title="Chicago Blackhawks">Chicago Blackhawks</a>. The Canadiens became only the second team in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NHL" title="NHL">NHL</a> history to win the Cup in game 7 on the road. This also marked the last NHL game that the late <a href="/wiki/Jean_B%C3%A9liveau" title="Jean Béliveau">Jean Béliveau</a> played.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_19" title="May 19">May 19</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mars_probe_program" title="Mars probe program">Mars probe program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Mars_2" title="Mars 2">Mars 2</a></i> is launched by the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_22" title="May 22">May 22</a> – An <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> lasting 20 seconds destroys most of <a href="/wiki/Bing%C3%B6l" title="Bingöl">Bingöl</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> – more than 1,000 are killed, 10,000 made homeless.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_23" title="May 23">May 23</a> – An air crash at <a href="/wiki/Rijeka_Airport" title="Rijeka Airport">Rijeka Airport</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a> kills 78 people, mostly British tourists.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a>
<ul>
<li>Austria and the People's Republic of China establish diplomatic relations.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Qantas" title="Qantas">Qantas</a> agrees to pay $500,000 to bomb hoaxer-extortionist Mr. Brown (Peter Macari), who is later arrested.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_27" title="May 27">May 27</a>
<ul>
<li>Six armed passengers hijack a <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romanian</a> passenger plane and force it to fly to <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christie%27s" title="Christie's">Christie's</a> auctions a diamond known as <a href="/wiki/Deepdene_(diamond)" title="Deepdene (diamond)">Deepdene</a>; it is later found to be artificially colored.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_28" title="May 28">May 28</a> – Portugal resigns from <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_30" title="May 30">May 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mariner_program" title="Mariner program">Mariner program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Mariner_9" title="Mariner 9">Mariner 9</a></i> is launched toward <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_31" title="May 31">May 31</a> – The birth of <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> is declared by the government in exile, in territory formerly part of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>June – <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a> passes its Chapter 766 laws enacting <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Special_Education" title="Special Education">Special Education</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a> – <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>: Vietnam Veterans for a Just Peace, claiming to represent the majority of U.S. veterans who served in <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a>, speak against war protests.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_6" title="June 6">June 6</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soyuz_program" title="Soyuz program">Soyuz program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Soyuz_11" title="Soyuz 11">Soyuz 11</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/Vladislav_Volkov" title="Vladislav Volkov">Vladislav Volkov</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Georgi_Dobrovolski" title="Georgi Dobrovolski">Georgi Dobrovolski</a>, <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Patsayev" title="Viktor Patsayev">Viktor Patsayev</a>) is launched.</li>
<li>A midair collision between <a href="/wiki/Hughes_Airwest_Flight_706" title="Hughes Airwest Flight 706">Hughes Airwest Flight 706</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Douglas_DC-9" title="Douglas DC-9">Douglas DC-9</a> jetliner and a U.S. Marine Corps <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/McDonnell_Douglas_F-4_Phantom" title="McDonnell Douglas F-4 Phantom">McDonnell Douglas F-4 Phantom</a> jet fighter near <a href="/wiki/Duarte,_California" title="Duarte, California">Duarte, California</a>, claims 50 lives.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_10" title="June 10">June 10</a>
<ul>
<li>The U.S. ends its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trade_embargo" title="Trade embargo">trade embargo</a> of China.</li>
<li>Corpus Thursday: A student rally on the streets of Mexico City is roughly dispersed.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_11" title="June 11">June 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Neville_Bonner" title="Neville Bonner">Neville Bonner</a> becomes the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indigenous_Australian" title="Indigenous Australian">Indigenous Australian</a> to sit in the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Australia" title="Parliament of Australia">Australian Parliament</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_13" title="June 13">June 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> begins to publish the <a href="/wiki/Pentagon_Papers" title="Pentagon Papers">Pentagon Papers</a>. <a class="external autonumber" href="http://usinfo.state.gov/usa/infousa/facts/democrac/48.htm" rel="nofollow">[1]</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Gijs_van_Lennep" title="Gijs van Lennep">Gijs van Lennep</a> (The Netherlands) and co-driver <a href="/wiki/Helmut_Marko" title="Helmut Marko">Helmut Marko</a> (Austria) win the <a href="/wiki/1971_24_Hours_of_Le_Mans" title="1971 24 Hours of Le Mans">24 Hours of Le Mans</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Martini_Racing" title="Martini Racing">Martini Racing</a> <a href="/wiki/Porsche_917" title="Porsche 917">Porsche 917</a>K.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_14" title="June 14">June 14</a> – Norway begins oil production in the <a href="/wiki/North_Sea" title="North Sea">North Sea</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_17" title="June 17">June 17</a>
<ul>
<li>Representatives of Japan and the United States sign the Okinawa Reversion Agreement, whereby the U.S. will return control of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Okinawa" title="Okinawa">Okinawa</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></li>
<li>President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a> declares the U.S. <a href="/wiki/War_on_Drugs" title="War on Drugs">War on Drugs</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_18" title="June 18">June 18</a> – <a href="/wiki/Southwest_Airlines" title="Southwest Airlines">Southwest Airlines</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Low-cost_carrier" title="Low-cost carrier">low-cost carrier</a>, begins its first flights between <a href="/wiki/Dallas" title="Dallas">Dallas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Houston" title="Houston">Houston</a>, and <a href="/wiki/San_Antonio" title="San Antonio">San Antonio</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_20" title="June 20">June 20</a> – Britain announces that Soviet space scientist Anatoli Fedoseyev has been granted asylum.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_21" title="June 21">June 21</a> – Britain begins new negotiations for <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Community" title="European Economic Community">EEC</a> membership in Luxembourg.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_25" title="June 25">June 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Madagascar" title="Madagascar">Madagascar</a> accuses the U.S. of being connected to the plot to oust the current government; the U.S. recalls its ambassador.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_27" title="June 27">June 27</a> – Concert promoter <a href="/wiki/Bill_Graham_(promoter)" title="Bill Graham (promoter)">Bill Graham</a> closes the legendary <a href="/wiki/Fillmore_East" title="Fillmore East">Fillmore East</a>, which first opened on 2nd Avenue (between 5th and 6th Streets) in New York City on March 8, 1968.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_28" title="June 28">June 28</a> – Assassin Jerome A. Johnson shoots <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Colombo" title="Joseph Colombo">Joe Colombo</a> in the head in a middle of an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian-American" title="Italian-American">Italian-American</a> rally, putting him in a coma.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_30" title="June 30">June 30</a>
<ul>
<li>After a successful mission aboard <i><a href="/wiki/Salyut_1" title="Salyut 1">Salyut 1</a></i>, the world's first manned space station, the crew of the <i><a href="/wiki/Soyuz_11" title="Soyuz 11">Soyuz 11</a></i> spacecraft are killed when their air supply leaks out through a faulty valve.</li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Times_Co._v._United_States" title="New York Times Co. v. United States">New York Times Co. v. United States</a></i>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Supreme_Court" title="U.S. Supreme Court">U.S. Supreme Court</a> rules that the <a href="/wiki/Pentagon_Papers" title="Pentagon Papers">Pentagon Papers</a> may be published, rejecting government injunctions as unconstitutional prior restraint.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>July – <a href="/wiki/Nordic_Council" title="Nordic Council">Nordic Council</a> secretariat inaugurated.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_3" title="July 3">July 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Jim_Morrison" title="Jim Morrison">Jim Morrison</a>, lead singer of <a href="/wiki/The_Doors" title="The Doors">The Doors</a> is found dead in his bathtub in Paris, France.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_4" title="July 4">July 4</a> – <a href="/wiki/Michael_S._Hart" title="Michael S. Hart">Michael S. Hart</a> posts the first <a href="/wiki/E-book" title="E-book">e-book</a>, a copy of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Declaration_of_Independence" title="United States Declaration of Independence">United States Declaration of Independence</a>, on the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Illinois_at_Urbana%E2%80%93Champaign" title="University of Illinois at Urbana–Champaign">University of Illinois at Urbana–Champaign</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Mainframe_computer" title="Mainframe computer">mainframe computer</a>, the origin of <a href="/wiki/Project_Gutenberg" title="Project Gutenberg">Project Gutenberg</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_5" title="July 5">July 5</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Right_to_vote" title="Right to vote">Right to vote</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/26th_Amendment_to_the_United_States_Constitution" title="26th Amendment to the United States Constitution">26th Amendment to the United States Constitution</a>, formally certified by President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a>, lowers the voting age from 21 to 18.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_6" title="July 6">July 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hastings_Banda" title="Hastings Banda">Hastings Banda</a> is proclaimed <a href="/wiki/President_for_Life" title="President for Life">President for Life</a> of <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a> – The United Kingdom increases its troops in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> to 11,000.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_10" title="July 10">July 10</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_11" title="July 11">July 11</a> – Coup attempt in <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a>: 1,400 cadets take over the king's palace for 3 hours and kill 28 people; 158 rebels die when the king's troops storm the palace (10 high-ranking officers are later executed for involvement).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_10" title="July 10">July 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Gloria_Steinem" title="Gloria Steinem">Gloria Steinem</a> makes her <a href="/wiki/Address_to_the_Women_of_America" title="Address to the Women of America">Address to the Women of America</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_11" title="July 11">July 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Copper" title="Copper">Copper</a> mines in <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> are nationalized.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_13" title="July 13">July 13</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%93lafur_J%C3%B3hannesson" title="Ólafur Jóhannesson">Ólafur Jóhannesson</a> forms a government in <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">Iceland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordanian</a> army troops launch an offensive against Palestinian guerillas in Jordan.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavian</a> government begins allowing foreign companies to take their profits from the country.</li>
<li>Paced by a prodigious home run by <a href="/wiki/Reggie_Jackson" title="Reggie Jackson">Reggie Jackson</a>, which hits a transformer on the roof of <a href="/wiki/Tiger_Stadium_(Detroit)" title="Tiger Stadium (Detroit)">Tiger Stadium</a>, the <a href="/wiki/American_League" title="American League">American League</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/National_League" title="National League">National League</a> 6-4 in the <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> All-Star Game in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Detroit,_Michigan" title="Detroit, Michigan">Detroit</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_14" title="July 14">July 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> severs its diplomatic ties with <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_15" title="July 15">July 15</a> – American President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a> announces his <a href="/wiki/1972_Nixon_visit_to_China" title="1972 Nixon visit to China">1972 visit to China</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">July 17</a> – Italy and Austria sign a treaty that ends the schism about <a href="/wiki/South_Tyrol" title="South Tyrol">South Tyrol</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_18" title="July 18">July 18</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Trucial_States" title="Trucial States">Trucial States</a> are formed in the <a href="/wiki/Persian_Gulf" title="Persian Gulf">Persian Gulf</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_19" title="July 19">July 19</a> – The South Tower of the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_(1973%E2%80%932001)" title="World Trade Center (1973–2001)">World Trade Center</a> is topped out at 1,362 feet (415 m), making it the second tallest building in the world.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_19" title="July 19">July 19</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_23" title="July 23">July 23</a> – Major Hashem al-Atta ousts Jaafar Muhammad al-Nimeiri in a military coup in <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a>. Fighting continues until on <a href="/wiki/July_22" title="July 22">July 22</a>, when pro-Nimeiri troops win. Al-Atta and 3 officers are executed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_24" title="July 24">July 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/Georgina_Rizk" title="Georgina Rizk">Georgina Rizk</a> of <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a> will crown <a href="/wiki/Miss_Universe_1971" title="Miss Universe 1971">Miss Universe 1971</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_25" title="July 25">July 25</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_30" title="July 30">July 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Arturo_Benedetti_Michelangeli" title="Arturo Benedetti Michelangeli">Arturo Benedetti Michelangeli</a> records in <a href="/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">Munich</a> two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Debussy" title="Debussy">Debussy</a> works for <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Grammophon" title="Deutsche Grammophon">Deutsche Grammophon</a>; it's his fifth recording.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_26" title="July 26">July 26</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">Apollo 15</a></i> (carrying astronauts <a href="/wiki/David_Scott" title="David Scott">David Scott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alfred_Worden" title="Alfred Worden">Alfred Worden</a>, and <a href="/wiki/James_Irwin" title="James Irwin">James Irwin</a>) is launched.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_28" title="July 28">July 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Abdel_Khaliq_Mahjub" title="Abdel Khaliq Mahjub">Abdel Khaliq Mahjub</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudanese</a> communist leader, is hanged.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_29" title="July 29">July 29</a> – The United Kingdom opts out of the <a href="/wiki/Space_Race" title="Space Race">Space Race</a>, with the cancellation of its <a href="/wiki/Black_Arrow" title="Black Arrow">Black Arrow</a> launch vehicle.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_30" title="July 30">July 30</a> – In Japan, an <a href="/wiki/All_Nippon_Airways" title="All Nippon Airways">All Nippon Airways</a> <a href="/wiki/Boeing_727" title="Boeing 727">Boeing 727</a> collides with a Japanese fighter jet; 162 people are killed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_31" title="July 31">July 31</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">Apollo 15</a></i> astronauts <a href="/wiki/David_Scott" title="David Scott">David Scott</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Irwin" title="James Irwin">James Irwin</a> become the first to ride in a <a href="/wiki/Lunar_rover" title="Lunar rover">lunar rover</a>, a day after landing on the Moon.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>August – <a href="/wiki/Camden,_New_Jersey" title="Camden, New Jersey">Camden, New Jersey</a> erupts in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Race_riot" title="Race riot">race riots</a> following the beating death of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puerto_Rican_people" title="Puerto Rican people">Puerto Rican</a> motorist by city police. Looting and arson occurred. This is a turning point in Camden's decline to one of the poorest and highest-crime municipalities in the United States. Camden was, however, the site of a 1949 shooting rampage by <a href="/wiki/Howard_Unruh" title="Howard Unruh">Howard Unruh</a>, considered by some to be the first <a href="/wiki/Mass_murder" title="Mass murder">mass murderer</a> in the United States. The riots result in the demise of Camden's <a href="/wiki/Sears" title="Sears">Sears</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Great_Atlantic_%26_Pacific_Tea_Company" title="The Great Atlantic &amp; Pacific Tea Company">A&amp;P</a> branches. Also in 1971, <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia_International_Records" title="Philadelphia International Records">Philadelphia International Records</a> is established, with Camden native Leon Huff as co-founder.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_1" title="August 1">August 1</a> – In New York City, 40,000 attend <a href="/wiki/The_Concert_for_Bangladesh" title="The Concert for Bangladesh">The Concert for Bangladesh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_2" title="August 2">August 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/J._C._Penney" title="J. C. Penney">J. C. Penney</a> debuts its trademark <a href="/wiki/Helvetica" title="Helvetica">Helvetica</a> wordmark which has been used ever since.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_5" title="August 5">August 5</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Pacific_Forum" title="South Pacific Forum">South Pacific Forum</a> (SPF) is established.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_6" title="August 6">August 6</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Lunar_eclipse" title="Lunar eclipse">lunar eclipse</a> lasting 1 hour, 40 minutes, and 4 seconds is observed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_7" title="August 7">August 7</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">Apollo 15</a></i> returns to <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_9" title="August 9">August 9</a>
<ul>
<li>India signs a 20-year treaty of friendship and cooperation with the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Internment" title="Internment">Internment</a> in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>: British security forces arrest hundreds of <a href="/wiki/Irish_nationalism" title="Irish nationalism">nationalists</a> and detain them without trial in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maze_(HM_Prison)" title="Maze (HM Prison)">Long Kesh</a> prison; 20 people die in the riots that follow.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_11" title="August 11">August 11</a> – Construction begins on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Louisiana_Superdome" title="Louisiana Superdome">Louisiana Superdome</a> in <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">New Orleans</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_12" title="August 12">August 12</a>
<ul>
<li>Three thousand people from <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">Belfast</a> and <a href="/wiki/Derry" title="Derry">Derry</a> flee to the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Republic of Ireland</a> because of the violence.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> severs diplomatic relations with <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a> because of border clashes.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_14" title="August 14">August 14</a>
<ul>
<li>British troops are stationed on the Ireland border to stop arms smuggling.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a> declares independence as the State of Bahrain (Kingdom of Bahrain as of February 2002).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_15" title="August 15">August 15</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jackie_Stewart" title="Jackie Stewart">Jackie Stewart</a> becomes <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a> World Drivers' Champion in the <a href="/wiki/Tyrrell_Racing" title="Tyrrell Racing">Tyrrell</a> <a href="/wiki/Tyrrell_003" title="Tyrrell 003">003</a>-<a href="/wiki/Cosworth" title="Cosworth">Cosworth</a>.</li>
<li>The number of British troops in Northern Ireland is raised to 12,500.</li>
<li>President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a> announces that the United States will no longer convert dollars to gold at a fixed value, effectively ending the <a href="/wiki/Bretton_Woods_system" title="Bretton Woods system">Bretton Woods system</a>. He also imposes a 90-day freeze on wages, prices and rents.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_18" title="August 18">August 18</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>: Australia and New Zealand decide to withdraw their troops from <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>.</li>
<li>British troops are engaged in a firefight with the <a href="/wiki/Irish_Republican_Army" title="Irish Republican Army">IRA</a> in <a href="/wiki/Derry" title="Derry">Derry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_19" title="August 19">August 19</a>–<a href="/wiki/August_22" title="August 22">August 22</a> – A right-wing coup ignites a rebellion in <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>. Miners and students join troops to support president <a href="/wiki/Juan_Jos%C3%A9_Torres" title="Juan José Torres">Juan José Torres</a>, but eventually <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Banzer" title="Hugo Banzer">Hugo Banzer</a> takes over.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_20" title="August 20">August 20</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/International_Telecommunications_Satellite_Organization" title="International Telecommunications Satellite Organization">International Telecommunications Satellite Organization</a> (Intelsat) (effective 12 February 1973).</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/USS_Manatee_(AO-58)" title="USS Manatee (AO-58)">USS Manatee (AO-58)</a> spills 1,000 US gallons (3,800 L) of fuel oil on <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">President Nixon</a>'s Western White House beach in <a href="/wiki/San_Clemente,_California" title="San Clemente, California">San Clemente, California</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_21" title="August 21">August 21</a> – A bomb made of two hand grenades by communist rebels explodes in the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_(Philippines)" title="Liberal Party (Philippines)">Liberal Party</a> campaign party in <a href="/wiki/Plaza_Miranda_bombing" title="Plaza Miranda bombing">Plaza Miranda</a> in <a href="/wiki/Quiapo,_Manila" title="Quiapo, Manila">Quiapo, Manila</a> the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, injuring several anti-<a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Marcos" title="Ferdinand Marcos">Marcos</a> political candidates.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_25" title="August 25">August 25</a>
<ul>
<li>Border clashes occur between <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a> and <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> and eastern <a href="/wiki/Bengal" title="Bengal">Bengal</a> are flooded; thousands flee the area.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_26" title="August 26">August 26</a> – A civilian government takes power in Greece.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_30" title="August 30">August 30</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Progressive_Conservative_Association_of_Alberta" title="Progressive Conservative Association of Alberta">Progressive Conservatives</a> under <a href="/wiki/Peter_Lougheed" title="Peter Lougheed">Peter Lougheed</a> defeat the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Social_Credit_Party_of_Alberta" title="Social Credit Party of Alberta">Social Credit</a> government under <a href="/wiki/Harry_Strom" title="Harry Strom">Harry E. Strom</a> in a <a href="/wiki/General_election" title="General election">general election</a>, ending 36 years of uninterrupted power for Social Credit in <a href="/wiki/Alberta" title="Alberta">Alberta</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>September – <a href="/wiki/Operation_Sourisak_Montry_VIII" title="Operation Sourisak Montry VIII">Operation Sourisak Montry VIII</a> opens when forces of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Thai_Army" title="Royal Thai Army">Royal Thai Army</a> recapture several positions in the territory of <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a> on the south bank of the <a href="/wiki/Mekong" title="Mekong">Mekong</a> in response to an encroaching Chinese presence to the north.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_3" title="September 3">September 3</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a> gains independence from the United Kingdom. Unlike most nearby <a href="/wiki/Emirate" title="Emirate">emirates</a>, Qatar declines to become part of either the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> or <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Manlio_Brosio" title="Manlio Brosio">Manlio Brosio</a> resigns as <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> Secretary General.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_4" title="September 4">September 4</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Boeing_727" title="Boeing 727">Boeing 727</a> (<a href="/wiki/Alaska_Airlines_Flight_1866" title="Alaska Airlines Flight 1866">Alaska Airlines Flight 1866</a>) crashes into the side of a mountain near <a href="/wiki/Juneau,_Alaska" title="Juneau, Alaska">Juneau, Alaska</a>, killing all 111 people on board.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_8" title="September 8">September 8</a> – In Washington, D.C., the <a href="/wiki/John_F._Kennedy_Center_for_the_Performing_Arts" title="John F. Kennedy Center for the Performing Arts">John F. Kennedy Center for the Performing Arts</a> is inaugurated, with the opening feature being the premiere of <a href="/wiki/Leonard_Bernstein" title="Leonard Bernstein">Leonard Bernstein</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Mass_(Bernstein)" title="Mass (Bernstein)">Mass</a></i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_9" title="September 9">September 9</a> – <a href="/wiki/September_13" title="September 13">September 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Attica_Prison_riot" title="Attica Prison riot">Attica Prison riot</a>: – A revolt breaks out at the maximum-security prison in <a href="/wiki/Attica_(town),_New_York" title="Attica (town), New York">Attica, New York</a>. In the end, <a href="/wiki/State_police" title="State police">state police</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_National_Guard" title="United States National Guard">United States National Guard</a> storm the facility; 42 are killed, 10 of them hostages.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_19" title="September 19">September 19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Trams_in_Ballarat" title="Trams in Ballarat">Trams in Ballarat</a> (Victoria, Australia) cease to run.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_21" title="September 21">September 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> – Britain expels 90 KGB and GRU officials; 15 are not allowed to return.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_27" title="September 27">September 27</a>–<a href="/wiki/October_11" title="October 11">October 11</a> – Japanese Emperor <a href="/wiki/Hirohito" title="Hirohito">Hirohito</a> travels abroad.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_28" title="September 28">September 28</a> – <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">Cardinal</a> <a href="/wiki/J%C3%B3zsef_Mindszenty" title="József Mindszenty">József Mindszenty</a>, who has taken refuge in the U.S. Embassy in <a href="/wiki/Budapest" title="Budapest">Budapest</a> since <a href="/wiki/1956" title="1956">1956</a>, is allowed to leave Hungary.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_29" title="September 29">September 29</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Cyclone" title="Cyclone">cyclone</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Bengal" title="Bay of Bengal">Bay of Bengal</a>, in the Indian state of <a href="/wiki/Odisha" title="Odisha">Odisha</a>, kills 10,000.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_1" title="October 1">October 1</a> – <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_World" title="Walt Disney World">Walt Disney World</a> opens in <a href="/wiki/Orlando,_Florida" title="Orlando, Florida">Orlando, Florida</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_14" title="October 14">October 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Greenpeace" title="Greenpeace">Greenpeace</a> is founded in Vancouver, British Columbia, Canada.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_18" title="October 18">October 18</a> – In New York City, the <a href="/wiki/Knapp_Commission" title="Knapp Commission">Knapp Commission</a> begins public hearings on police corruption.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_21" title="October 21">October 21</a>
<ul>
<li>U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a> nominates <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lewis_Franklin_Powell,_Jr." title="Lewis Franklin Powell, Jr.">Lewis Franklin Powell, Jr.</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/William_H._Rehnquist" title="William H. Rehnquist">William H. Rehnquist</a> to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Supreme_Court" title="U.S. Supreme Court">U.S. Supreme Court</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Clarkston_explosion" title="Clarkston explosion">Clarkston explosion</a> in Scotland kills 22 people.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a> – The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> admits the People's Republic of China and expels the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (or Taiwan).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_27" title="October 27">October 27</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> is renamed <a href="/wiki/Zaire" title="Zaire">Zaire</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_28" title="October 28">October 28</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">House of Commons of the United Kingdom</a> votes 356–244 in favour of joining the <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Community" title="European Economic Community">European Economic Community</a>.</li>
<li>The United Kingdom becomes the sixth nation successfully to launch a satellite into orbit using its own <a href="/wiki/Launch_vehicle" title="Launch vehicle">launch vehicle</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prospero_(satellite)" title="Prospero (satellite)">Prospero</a> (X-3) experimental communications satellite, using a <a href="/wiki/Black_Arrow" title="Black Arrow">Black Arrow</a> carrier rocket from <a href="/wiki/Woomera,_South_Australia" title="Woomera, South Australia">Woomera, South Australia</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Khedivial_Opera_House" title="Khedivial Opera House">Khedivial Opera House</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> (Egypt) burns down.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_29" title="October 29">October 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a> – <a href="/wiki/Vietnamization" title="Vietnamization">Vietnamization</a>: The total number of American troops still in <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> drops to a record low of 196,700 (the lowest since January 1966).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_30" title="October 30">October 30</a> – Rev. <a href="/wiki/Ian_Paisley" title="Ian Paisley">Ian Paisley</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Unionist_Party" title="Democratic Unionist Party">Democratic Unionist Party</a> is founded in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_31" title="October 31">October 31</a> – A bomb explodes at the top of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Post_Office_Tower" title="Post Office Tower">Post Office Tower</a> in London.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_3" title="November 3">November 3</a> – The <i><a href="/wiki/Unix" title="Unix">UNIX</a> Programmer's Manual</i> is published.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_6" title="November 6">November 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Operation_Grommet" title="Operation Grommet">Operation Grommet</a>: The U.S. tests a thermonuclear warhead at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amchitka_Island" title="Amchitka Island">Amchitka Island</a> in Alaska, code-named Project Cannikin. At around 5 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Megatons" title="Megatons">megatons</a>, it is the largest ever U.S. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Underground_nuclear_testing" title="Underground nuclear testing">underground detonation</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_8" title="November 8">November 8</a> – Led Zeppelin releases their Fourth Studio album "Led Zeppelin IV", which goes on to sell 23,000,000 copies.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_9" title="November 9">November 9</a> – A <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/C-130" title="C-130">C-130</a> crashes into the <a href="/wiki/Ligurian_Sea" title="Ligurian Sea">Ligurian Sea</a> near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Leghorn,_Italy" title="Leghorn, Italy">Leghorn, Italy</a>, killing all 51 people on board.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_10" title="November 10">November 10</a> – In <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Khmer_Rouge" title="Khmer Rouge">Khmer Rouge</a> forces attack <a href="/wiki/Phnom_Penh" title="Phnom Penh">Phnom Penh</a> and its airport, killing 44, wounding at least 30 and damaging 9 <a href="/wiki/Airplane" title="Airplane">airplanes</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_12" title="November 12">November 12</a> – Vietnam War – <a href="/wiki/Vietnamization" title="Vietnamization">Vietnamization</a>: U.S. President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Richard_M._Nixon" title="Richard M. Nixon">Richard M. Nixon</a> sets February 1, 1972, as the deadline for the removal of another 45,000 American troops from <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_13" title="November 13">November 13</a> – <a href="/wiki/Mariner_program" title="Mariner program">Mariner program</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Mariner_9" title="Mariner 9">Mariner 9</a></i> becomes the first spacecraft to enter <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a> orbit successfully.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_14" title="November 14">November 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pope_Shenouda_III_of_Alexandria" title="Pope Shenouda III of Alexandria">Pope Shenouda III of Alexandria</a> is enthroned.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_15" title="November 15">November 15</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Intel" title="Intel">Intel</a> releases the world's first <a href="/wiki/Microprocessor" title="Microprocessor">microprocessor</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Intel_4004" title="Intel 4004">Intel 4004</a>.</li>
<li>International Organization and System of Space Communications (<a href="/wiki/Intersputnik" title="Intersputnik">Intersputnik</a>) (effective 12 July 1972).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_20" title="November 20">November 20</a> – A bridge still in construction, called Elevado Engenheiro Freyssinet, falls over the Paulo de Frontin Avenue, in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>; 48 people are killed and several injured. Reconstructed, the bridge is currently a part of the Linha Vermelha elevate.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_23" title="November 23">November 23</a> – The People's Republic of China takes the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a>'s seat on the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> (see <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">China and the United Nations</a>).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_24" title="November 24">November 24</a>
<ul>
<li>During a severe storm over <a href="/wiki/Washington_(state)" title="Washington (state)">Washington</a> State, a man calling himself <a href="/wiki/D._B._Cooper" title="D. B. Cooper">D. B. Cooper</a> parachutes from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Northwest_Orient_Airlines" title="Northwest Orient Airlines">Northwest Orient Airlines</a> plane he'd just hijacked, with US$200,000 in ransom money, and is never seen again (as of March 2008, this case remains the only unsolved skyjacking in history).</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> court sentences pretender <a href="/wiki/Alexis_Brimeyer" title="Alexis Brimeyer">Alexis Brimeyer</a> to 18 months in jail for falsely using a noble title; Brimeyer has already fled to Greece.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_28" title="November 28">November 28</a> – The 59th <a href="/wiki/Grey_Cup" title="Grey Cup">Grey Cup</a> Game sees the <a href="/wiki/Calgary_Stampeders" title="Calgary Stampeders">Calgary Stampeders</a> beat the <a href="/wiki/Toronto_Argonauts" title="Toronto Argonauts">Toronto Argonauts</a> 14-11.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_1" title="December 1">December 1</a> – <a href="/wiki/Cambodian_Civil_War" title="Cambodian Civil War">Cambodian Civil War</a>: <a href="/wiki/Khmer_Rouge" title="Khmer Rouge">Khmer Rouge</a> rebels intensify assaults on <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodian</a> government positions, forcing their retreat from Kompong Thmar and nearby Ba Ray, 10 kilometers northeast of <a href="/wiki/Phnom_Penh" title="Phnom Penh">Phnom Penh</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_2" title="December 2">December 2</a> – Six <a href="/wiki/Persian_Gulf" title="Persian Gulf">Persian Gulf</a> sheikdoms found the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_3" title="December 3">December 3</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Indo-Pakistani_War_of_1971" title="Indo-Pakistani War of 1971">Indo-Pakistani War of 1971</a> begins with <a href="/wiki/Operation_Chengiz_Khan" title="Operation Chengiz Khan">Operation Chengiz Khan</a> as Pakistan launches preemptive attacks on nine Indian airbases. The next day India launches a massive invasion of East Pakistan.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_3" title="December 3">December 3</a>–<a href="/wiki/December_4" title="December 4">4</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> <a href="/wiki/Submarine" title="Submarine">submarine</a> <a href="/wiki/PNS_Ghazi" title="PNS Ghazi">PNS <i>Ghazi</i></a> (former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USS_Diablo" title="USS Diablo">USS <i>Diablo</i></a>) sinks mysteriously near the Indian coast while laying mines.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_4" title="December 4">December 4</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Montreux" title="Montreux">Montreux</a> Casino burns down during a <a href="/wiki/Frank_Zappa" title="Frank Zappa">Frank Zappa</a> concert (the event is memorialized in the <a href="/wiki/Deep_Purple" title="Deep Purple">Deep Purple</a> song "<a href="/wiki/Smoke_on_the_Water" title="Smoke on the Water">Smoke on the Water</a>"). The casino is rebuilt in <a href="/wiki/1975" title="1975">1975</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/McGurk%27s_Bar_bombing" title="McGurk's Bar bombing">McGurk's Bar bombing</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Ulster_Volunteer_Force" title="Ulster Volunteer Force">Ulster Volunteer Force</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">Belfast</a> kills 15.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_8" title="December 8">December 8</a> – U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Richard Nixon</a> orders the 7th Fleet to move towards the Bay of Bengal in the Indian Ocean.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_10" title="December 10">December 10</a> – The <a href="/wiki/John_Sinclair_Freedom_Rally" title="John Sinclair Freedom Rally">John Sinclair Freedom Rally</a> in support of the imprisoned activist features a performance by <a href="/wiki/John_Lennon" title="John Lennon">John Lennon</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crisler_Arena" title="Crisler Arena">Crisler Arena</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ann_Arbor,_Michigan" title="Ann Arbor, Michigan">Ann Arbor, Michigan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_11" title="December 11">December 11</a> – <a href="/wiki/Nihat_Erim" title="Nihat Erim">Nihat Erim</a> forms the new government of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> (34th government; Nihat Erim has served two times as prime minister).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_16" title="December 16">December 16</a> – <i>Victory Day of Bangladesh</i>: The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan Army</a> in <a href="/wiki/East_Pakistan" title="East Pakistan">East Pakistan</a> (now <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>) surrenders to the freedom fighters of Bangladesh, ending the <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Liberation_War" title="Bangladesh Liberation War">Bangladesh Liberation War</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_18" title="December 18">December 18</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._dollar" title="U.S. dollar">U.S. dollar</a> is devalued for the second time in history.</li>
<li>The world's largest <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hydroelectric_plant" title="Hydroelectric plant">hydroelectric plant</a> in <a href="/wiki/Krasnoyarsk" title="Krasnoyarsk">Krasnoyarsk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>, begins operations.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Clube_Atl%C3%A9tico_Mineiro" title="Clube Atlético Mineiro">Clube Atlético Mineiro</a> wins the Brazil Football Championship.</li>
<li>Intelsat IV (F3) is launched; it enters commercial service over the Atlantic Ocean February 18, 1972.</li>
<li>The controversial dystopian crime film <i><a href="/wiki/A_Clockwork_Orange_(film)" title="A Clockwork Orange (film)">A Clockwork Orange</a></i> directed by <a href="/wiki/Stanley_Kubrick" title="Stanley Kubrick">Stanley Kubrick</a> is released in New York City.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_20" title="December 20">December 20</a> – Two groups of French doctors involved in <a href="/wiki/Humanitarian_aid" title="Humanitarian aid">humanitarian aid</a> merge to form <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="Médecins Sans Frontières">Médecins Sans Frontières</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">December 24</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Giovanni_Leone" title="Giovanni Leone">Giovanni Leone</a> is elected <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_the_Italian_Republic" title="President of the Italian Republic">President of the Italian Republic</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juliane_Koepcke" title="Juliane Koepcke">Juliane Koepcke</a> survives a fall of 10,000 feet following disintegration of <a href="/wiki/LANSA_Flight_508" title="LANSA Flight 508">LANSA Flight 508</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_25" title="December 25">December 25</a>
<ul>
<li>In the longest <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a> game in <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> history, the <a href="/wiki/Miami_Dolphins" title="Miami Dolphins">Miami Dolphins</a> beat the <a href="/wiki/Kansas_City_Chiefs" title="Kansas City Chiefs">Kansas City Chiefs</a>.</li>
<li>A fire at a 22-story hotel in <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a>, South Korea kills 158 people.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_29" title="December 29">December 29</a> – The United Kingdom gives up its military bases in <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ray_Tomlinson" title="Ray Tomlinson">Ray Tomlinson</a> sends the first <a href="/wiki/ARPANET" title="ARPANET">ARPANET</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/E-mail" title="E-mail">e-mail</a> between host computers.</li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Free_State_of_Christiania" title="Free State of Christiania">Free State of Christiania</a> is founded.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Seychelles_International_Airport" title="Seychelles International Airport">Seychelles International Airport</a> in <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Seychelles" title="Victoria, Seychelles">Victoria, Seychelles</a> (<a href="/wiki/Mah%C3%A9,_Seychelles" title="Mahé, Seychelles">Mahe</a>) is completed.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Crude_oil" title="Crude oil">Crude oil</a> production peaks in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Continental_United_States" title="Continental United States">continental United States</a> at approximately 4.5 million barrels per day (720,000 m<sup>3</sup>/d).</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Center_for_Science_in_the_Public_Interest" title="Center for Science in the Public Interest">Center for Science in the Public Interest</a> is established.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Institute_on_Alcohol_Abuse_and_Alcoholism" title="National Institute on Alcohol Abuse and Alcoholism">National Institute on Alcohol Abuse and Alcoholism</a> is established.</li>
<li>The British crime magazine <i>Master Detective</i>, in an attempt to capitalize on the <a href="/wiki/Murder_of_Diane_Maxwell" title="Murder of Diane Maxwell">murder of Diane Maxwell</a>, illegally takes photo negatives from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houston,_Texas" title="Houston, Texas">Houston, Texas</a> and uses them for a 1971 edition.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kamuzu_Banda" title="Kamuzu Banda">Kamuzu Banda</a>, president of <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a>, becomes the first Black President to visit South Africa.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Births">Births</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1971&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Births">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
